This report was auto-generated by executing local Django API routes with Django test client.

Authentication was not provided (Bearer placeholder only in request examples), so protected endpoints return 401/403/302 as expected.

```json
{
```

## Endpoint Body Templates (Use In Postman/Mobile)

These are endpoint-specific payloads for write APIs (create/update/delete/status/toggle).

### 1. Auth APIs

`POST /api/auth/login/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `mobile`, `password`

```json
{
  "mobile": "9876543210",
  "password": "YourPassword123"
}
```

`POST /api/auth/logout/` (`application/json`)

Optional fields: `refresh`

```json
{
  "refresh": "eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOi..."
}
```

`POST /api/auth/forgot-password/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `email`

```json
{
  "email": "buyer@example.com"
}
```

`POST /api/auth/change-password/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `old_password`, `new_password`, `confirm_password`

```json
{
  "old_password": "OldPass123",
  "new_password": "NewPass123",
  "confirm_password": "NewPass123"
}
```

`POST /api/auth/register/` (`multipart/form-data`)

Required fields: `mobile`, `email`, `first_name`, `role`, `adharcard_image`  
Optional fields: `last_name`, `pan_number`, `gst_number`, `gender`, `dob`, `pan_image`, `gst_image`, `shopact_image`

```json
{
  "mobile": "9876543210",
  "email": "newuser@example.com",
  "first_name": "Ravi",
  "last_name": "Sharma",
  "role": "seller",
  "pan_number": "ABCDE1234F",
  "gst_number": "27ABCDE1234F1Z5",
  "gender": "male",
  "dob": "1995-06-10",
  "adharcard_image": "<file>",
  "pan_image": "<file>",
  "gst_image": "<file>",
  "shopact_image": "<file>"
}
```

### 2. User Creation/Update APIs

`POST /api/adduser/` (`multipart/form-data`, admin/super-admin)

Required fields: `mobile`, `email`, `first_name`, `role`, `adharcard_image`, `tag_ids` (1-15)  
Optional fields: `last_name`, `pan_number`, `gst_number`, `gender`, `dob`, `pan_image`, `gst_image`, `shopact_image`

```json
{
  "mobile": "9988776655",
  "email": "seller1@example.com",
  "first_name": "Amit",
  "last_name": "Patel",
  "role": "seller",
  "pan_number": "ABCDE1234F",
  "gst_number": "27ABCDE1234F1Z5",
  "gender": "male",
  "dob": "1992-01-15",
  "tag_ids": [1, 2],
  "adharcard_image": "<file>",
  "pan_image": "<file>",
  "gst_image": "<file>",
  "shopact_image": "<file>"
}
```

`POST /api/users/create/` (`multipart/form-data` recommended, admin/super-admin)

Required fields: `email`, `mobile`, `password`, `role`, `pan_image`, `tag_ids` (1-15)  
Optional fields: `first_name`, `last_name`, `pan_number`, `gst_number`, `char_password`, `gst_image`, `shopact_image`, `adharcard_image`

```json
{
  "email": "buyer1@example.com",
  "mobile": "9123456789",
  "password": "Pass@1234",
  "char_password": "Pass@1234",
  "first_name": "Neha",
  "last_name": "Jain",
  "role": "buyer",
  "pan_number": "ABCDE1234F",
  "gst_number": "27ABCDE1234F1Z5",
  "tag_ids": [3, 5],
  "pan_image": "<file>",
  "gst_image": "<file>",
  "shopact_image": "<file>",
  "adharcard_image": "<file>"
}
```

`POST /api/users/<int:user_id>/update/` (`application/json`, admin/super-admin)

Required fields: `email`, `mobile`  
Recommended: `role`  
Optional fields: `first_name`, `last_name`, `pan_number`, `gst_number`, `char_password`, `tag_ids`

```json
{
  "email": "buyer1.updated@example.com",
  "mobile": "9123456789",
  "first_name": "Neha",
  "last_name": "Jain",
  "role": "buyer",
  "pan_number": "ABCDE1234F",
  "gst_number": "27ABCDE1234F1Z5",
  "char_password": "Pass@1234",
  "tag_ids": [3, 6]
}
```

`POST /api/users/<int:user_id>/status/` (`application/json`, admin/super-admin)

Required fields: `status` (`active` | `deactivated` | `suspended`)  
Conditionally required: `suspension_reason` when `status = suspended`

```json
{
  "status": "suspended",
  "suspension_reason": "KYC mismatch"
}
```

`POST /api/users/<int:user_id>/delete/` (`application/json`)

Body not required:

```json
{}
```

### 3. Profile/KYC/Admin Tag APIs

`PATCH /api/profile/update/` (`application/json` or `multipart/form-data`)

Allowed fields: `first_name`, `last_name`, `email`, `mobile`, `profile_image`  
Admin-only extra fields: `pan_number`, `gst_number`, `gender`, `dob`

```json
{
  "first_name": "Ravi",
  "last_name": "Sharma",
  "email": "ravi@example.com",
  "mobile": "9876543210"
}
```

`POST /api/user/profile-image/` (`multipart/form-data`)

Required fields: `profile_image`

```json
{
  "profile_image": "<file>"
}
```

`POST /api/kyc/<int:user_id>/approve/` (`application/json`)

Body not required:

```json
{}
```

`POST /api/kyc/<int:user_id>/reject/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `rejection_reason`

```json
{
  "rejection_reason": "Document is unclear"
}
```

`POST /api/admin/tag/create/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `tag_name`

```json
{
  "tag_name": "Premium Buyer"
}
```

`POST /api/admin/tag/<int:tag_id>/update/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `tag_name`

```json
{
  "tag_name": "Updated Tag Name"
}
```

`POST /api/admin/tag/<int:tag_id>/delete/` (`application/json`)

Body not required:

```json
{}
```

### 4. Offer/Product APIs (Mobile)

`POST /api/offers/create/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `title`, `category_id`, `amount`, `loading_from`, `loading_to`  
Admin-only required: `seller_id`  
Optional fields: `description`, `remark`, `brand_id`, `amount_unit`, `quantity`, `quantity_unit`

```json
{
  "title": "Cashew A Grade",
  "category_id": 1,
  "seller_id": 53,
  "amount": "340.00",
  "amount_unit": "ton",
  "quantity": "120.00",
  "quantity_unit": "ton",
  "loading_from": "Bhopal",
  "loading_to": "Nagpure",
  "remark": "Dispatch in 2 days",
  "description": "Fresh lot",
  "brand_id": 1
}
```

`POST /api/offers/<int:product_id>/update/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `title`, `category_id`, `amount`, `loading_from`, `loading_to`  
Optional fields: `description`, `remark`, `brand_id`, `amount_unit`, `loading_location`, `is_active`, `seller_id`

```json
{
  "title": "Cashew A Grade (Updated)",
  "category_id": 1,
  "seller_id": 53,
  "amount": "345.00",
  "amount_unit": "ton",
  "loading_from": "2026-03-01",
  "loading_to": "2026-03-05",
  "loading_location": "2026-03-01 -> 2026-03-05",
  "remark": "Updated remark",
  "description": "Updated lot",
  "brand_id": 1,
  "is_active": true
}
```

`POST /api/offers/<int:product_id>/toggle/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `is_active`

```json
{
  "is_active": true
}
```

`POST /api/offers/<int:product_id>/update-stock/` (`application/json`)

Required fields: `quantity`  
Optional fields: `mode` (`add` or `replace`)

```json
{
  "mode": "add",
  "quantity": "5.00"
}
```

`POST /api/offers/<int:product_id>/delete/` (`application/json`)

Body not required:

```json
{}
```

### 5. Contract APIs (Mobile)

`PATCH /api/mobile/contracts/<int:contract_id>/` (`application/json`, admin/super-admin only)

Allowed fields: `status`, `admin_remark`  
Valid `status`: `active`, `completed`, `cancelled`

```json
{
  "status": "completed",
  "admin_remark": "Deal closed successfully"
}
```

### 6. Branch APIs (Mobile)

`POST /api/branch/create/` (`application/json`, admin/super-admin)

Required fields: `location_name`, `state`, `city`, `area`  
Optional fields: `is_active`

```json
{
  "location_name": "Bhopal Main Branch",
  "state": "Madhya Pradesh",
  "city": "Bhopal",
  "area": "MP Nagar",
  "is_active": true
}
```

`POST /api/branch/update/<int:branch_id>/` (`application/json`, admin/super-admin)

Required fields: `location_name`, `state`, `city`, `area`  
Optional fields: `is_active`

```json
{
  "location_name": "Bhopal Branch Updated",
  "state": "Madhya Pradesh",
  "city": "Bhopal",
  "area": "Arera Colony",
  "is_active": true
}
```

`POST /api/branch/toggle/<int:branch_id>/` (`application/json`, admin/super-admin)

Optional fields: `is_active`

```json
{
  "is_active": false
}
```

`POST /api/branch/delete/<int:branch_id>/` (`application/json`)

Body not required:

```json
{}
```

```json
  "brand_name": "Premium Agro",
  "status": "active"
}
```

```json
{
  "brand_name": "Premium Agro Updated",
  "status": "inactive"
```

```json
    "Allow": "GET, POST, HEAD, OPTIONS",
```
```json
    "Cache-Control": "no-store, no-cache, must-revalidate, max-age=0",
    "Pragma": "no-cache",
    "Expires": "0",
    "X-Frame-Options": "DENY",
    "Content-Length": "172",
    "Vary": "Cookie",
    "X-Content-Type-Options": "nosniff",
    "Referrer-Policy": "same-origin",
    "Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy": "same-origin"
  },
  "body": {
    "kind": "json",
    "data": {
      "detail": "Given token not valid for any token type",
      "code": "token_not_valid",
      "messages": [
        {
          "token_class": "AccessToken",
          "token_type": "access",
          "message": "Token is invalid"
        }
```

```json
    "Content-Length": "172",

    "Referrer-Policy": "same-origin",
    "Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy": "same-origin"
```

```json
  "route_pattern": "api/users/<int:user_id>/",
```

```json
  "status_code": 401,
```

```json
  "headers": {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Authorization": "Bearer <token>"
  },
  "body": {
    "field1": "value",
    "field2": "value"
  }
}
```

### Response Data (Primary test)

```json
{
  "status_code": 401,
  "headers": {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer realm=\"api\"",
    "Allow": "POST, OPTIONS",
    "X-Frame-Options": "DENY",
    "Content-Length": "172",
    "Vary": "Cookie",
    "X-Content-Type-Options": "nosniff",
    "Referrer-Policy": "same-origin",
    "Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy": "same-origin"
  },
  "body": {
    "kind": "json",
    "data": {
      "detail": "Given token not valid for any token type",
      "code": "token_not_valid",
      "messages": [
        {
          "token_class": "AccessToken",
          "token_type": "access",
          "message": "Token is invalid"
        }
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

### cURL (Postman equivalent)

```bash
curl -i -X POST 'http://localhost:8000/api/branch/create/' -H 'Content-Type: application/json' -H 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' -d '{"field1": "value", "field2": "value"}'
```
